2.1.1.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:generic-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:generic-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.GenericDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__GenericDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.2.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:generic-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:generic-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.GenericInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_GenericInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__GenericInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.4.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-warning/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-warning/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:generic-warning/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:generic-warning/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:generic-warning/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.GenericWarning.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__GenericWarning__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.7.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-config-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-config-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-config-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-config-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-config-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrConfigInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrConfigInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrConfigInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrConfigInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrConfigInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrConfigInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.9.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-kafka-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-kafka-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-kafka-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-kafka-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-kafka-info/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrKafkaInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrKafkaInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrKafkaInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrKafkaInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrKafkaInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrKafkaInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.11.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:schema-mgr-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:schema-mgr-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:schema-mgr-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:schema-mgr-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:schema-mgr-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.SchemaMgrError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_SchemaMgrError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__SchemaMgrError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_SchemaMgrError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_SchemaMgrError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_SchemaMgrError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.13.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrEventPublisherError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrEventPublisherError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrEventPublisherError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.16.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrOperdataError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrOperdataError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrOperdataError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrOperdataError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrOperdataError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrOperdataError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.18.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-account-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-account-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-account-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-account-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-account-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrAccountError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrAccountError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrAccountError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.20.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-mock-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-mock-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-mock-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-mock-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-mock-error/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrMockError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrMockError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrMockError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrMockError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrMockError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrMockError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.23.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umb-config-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umb-config-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umb-config-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umb-config-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umb-config-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbConfigDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbConfigDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbConfigDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbConfigDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbConfigDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbConfigDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.25.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-subscriber-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-subscriber-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-subscriber-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-subscriber-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-subscriber-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrSubscriberDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrSubscriberDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrSubscriberDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrSubscriberDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrSubscriberDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrSubscriberDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.27.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-event-publisher-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrEventPublisherDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrEventPublisherDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrEventPublisherDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrEventPublisherDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrEventPublisherDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrEventPublisherDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.29.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-operdata-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrOperdataDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrOperdataDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrOperdataDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrOperdataDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrOperdataDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrOperdataDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.32.1.3  container rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-publish-stats-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-publish-stats-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-publish-stats-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-publish-stats-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwumbmgr-log:umbmgr-publish-stats-debug/rwumbmgr-log:template_params/rwumbmgr-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rwumbmgr_log.YangNotif.RwumbmgrLog.UmbmgrPublishStatsDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwumbmgrLogYang.YangNotif_RwumbmgrLog_UmbmgrPublishStatsDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwumbmgrLog__YangNotif__RwumbmgrLog__UmbmgrPublishStatsDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrPublishStatsDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrPublishStatsDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwumbmgrLog_RwumbmgrLog_notif_UmbmgrPublishStatsDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
